layout/generic, and layout/style directories:\\n\\n## 1. Frame Construction\\n\\nFrame construction is the initial process that creates the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in `nsCSSFrameConstructor` (layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h and .cpp), which extends `nsFrameManager` (layout/base/nsFrameManager.h and .cpp). This component converts styled DOM nodes into layout frames, handling anonymous frame generation for tables, flex containers, and other special layout modes.\\n\\n## 2. Block Layout Reflow\\n\\nThe block layout reflow implements the CSS Block Formatting Context (BFC) and handles the reflow of block-level frames. Key components include:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame** (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h and .cpp): Implements the core block box reflow algorithm that processes lines of inline content and handles floats, margins, padding, and borders.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState** (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h and .cpp): Maintains state information during block reflow, including margin collapsing calculations, float management, and line iteration.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext** (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h and .cpp): A helper class that computes reflow for child block frames within a parent block container.\\n\\n- **nsFloatManager** (layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h and .cpp): Manages float positioning and reserves space for floated elements within blocks.\\n\\nInline content reflow is handled by:\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout** (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h and .cpp): Manages the layout of inline content within lines.\\n- **nsInlineFrame** (layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h and .cpp): Handles reflow of inline and inline-block frames.\\n- **nsLineBox** (layout/generic/nsLineBox.h and .cpp): Represents a single line of inline content.\\n\\n## 3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\n\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system tracks which frames need reflow and ensures efficient incremental reflow:\\n\\n- **PresShell** (layout/base/PresShell.h and .cpp): The presentation shell is the top-level reflow coordinator that manages the reflow tree and calls `FrameNeedsReflow()` to schedule frames for reflow.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager** (layout/style/RestyleManager.h and .cpp): Manages style changes and invalidation, with `ProcessRestyledFrames()` handling the frame invalidation chain triggered by style updates.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput** (layout/generic/ReflowInput.h and .cpp): Encapsulates all input parameters needed for reflow, including available space, containing block size, and parent reflow state.\\n\\n- **RetainedDisplayListBuilder** (layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.h and .cpp): Tracks frame invalidation information for incremental display list construction.\\n\\n- **nsFrameStateBits** (layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h): Defines frame state bits including `NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY`, `NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN`, and `NS_BLOCK_LOOK_FOR_DIRTY_FRAMES` that mark frames needing reflow.\\n\\n- **nsAutoLayoutPhase** (layout/base/nsAutoLayoutPhase.h and .cpp): Manages layout phase tracking to prevent conflicting layout operations.\\n\\n## Reflow Data Flow\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline follows this sequence:\\n\\n1. Style changes trigger `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()`\\n2. `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()` applies style changes and marks frames dirty\\n3. `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` adds frames to the reflow queue\\n4. `PresShell::DoReflow()` calls frame `Reflow()` methods top-down\\n5. `nsBlockFrame::Reflow()` processes block layout with `BlockReflowState`\\n6. `nsInlineFrame::Reflow()` and `nsLineLayout` handle inline reflow\\n7. Float positioning is managed via `nsFloatManager`\\n8. `PresShell::DidReflow()` clears dirty bits after successful reflow\\n9. `RetainedDisplayListBuilder` tracks invalidation for the next paint cycle\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes `ReflowOutput` for reflow results, `nsPresContext` for presentation context state, and `nsLayoutUtils` utility functions for layout calculations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":9898,"cache_read_input_tokens":82693,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":9898},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9baeded7-efd0-4f9d-aa34-f44f83edacc9","uuid":"d9b55b6a-d386-4a22-b012-38b211e146f0"}

\"RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Firefox CSS layout engine reflow pipeline consists of three interconnected components implemented across the layout/base, layout/generic, and layout/style directories:\\n\\n## 1. Frame Construction\\n\\nFrame construction is the initial process that creates the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in `nsCSSFrameConstructor` (layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h and .cpp), which extends `nsFrameManager` (layout/base/nsFrameManager.h and .cpp). This component converts styled DOM nodes into layout frames, handling anonymous frame generation for tables, flex containers, and other special layout modes.\\n\\n## 2. Block Layout Reflow\\n\\nThe block layout reflow implements the CSS Block Formatting Context (BFC) and handles the reflow of block-level frames. Key components include:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame** (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h and .cpp): Implements the core block box reflow algorithm that processes lines of inline content and handles floats, margins, padding, and borders.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState** (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h and .cpp): Maintains state information during block reflow, including margin collapsing calculations, float management, and line iteration.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext** (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h and .cpp): A helper class that computes reflow for child block frames within a parent block container.\\n\\n- **nsFloatManager** (layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h and .cpp): Manages float positioning and reserves space for floated elements within blocks.\\n\\nInline content reflow is handled by:\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout** (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h and .cpp): Manages the layout of inline content within lines.\\n- **nsInlineFrame** (layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h and .cpp): Handles reflow of inline and inline-block frames.\\n- **nsLineBox** (layout/generic/nsLineBox.h and .cpp): Represents a single line of inline content.\\n\\n## 3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\n\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system tracks which frames need reflow and ensures efficient incremental reflow:\\n\\n- **PresShell** (layout/base/PresShell.h and .cpp): The presentation shell is the top-level reflow coordinator that manages the reflow tree and calls `FrameNeedsReflow()` to schedule frames for reflow.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager** (layout/style/RestyleManager.h and .cpp): Manages style changes and invalidation, with `ProcessRestyledFrames()` handling the frame invalidation chain triggered by style updates.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput** (layout/generic/ReflowInput.h and .cpp): Encapsulates all input parameters needed for reflow, including available space, containing block size, and parent reflow state.\\n\\n- **RetainedDisplayListBuilder** (layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.h and .cpp): Tracks frame invalidation information for incremental display list construction.\\n\\n- **nsFrameStateBits** (layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h): Defines frame state bits including `NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY`, `NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN`, and `NS_BLOCK_LOOK_FOR_DIRTY_FRAMES` that mark frames needing reflow.\\n\\n- **nsAutoLayoutPhase** (layout/base/nsAutoLayoutPhase.h and .cpp): Manages layout phase tracking to prevent conflicting layout operations.\\n\\n## Reflow Data Flow\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline follows this sequence:\\n\\n1. Style changes trigger `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()`\\n2. `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()` applies style changes and marks frames dirty\\n3. `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` adds frames to the reflow queue\\n4. `PresShell::DoReflow()` calls frame `Reflow()` methods top-down\\n5. `nsBlockFrame::Reflow()` processes block layout with `BlockReflowState`\\n6. `nsInlineFrame::Reflow()` and `nsLineLayout` handle inline reflow\\n7. Float positioning is managed via `nsFloatManager`\\n8. `PresShell::DidReflow()` clears dirty bits after successful reflow\\n9. `RetainedDisplayListBuilder` tracks invalidation for the next paint cycle\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes `ReflowOutput` for reflow results, `nsPresContext` for presentation context state, and `nsLayoutUtils` utility functions for layout calculations.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
